from openpyxl import load_workbook
import sys

file_path = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else 'achievement250726.xlsx'

wb = load_workbook(file_path)
ws = wb.active

print(f"Sheet names: {wb.sheetnames}")
print(f"Active sheet: {ws.title}")
print(f"Max row: {ws.max_row}, Max col: {ws.max_column}")
print("\nFirst 10 rows:")

for i, row in enumerate(ws.iter_rows(values_only=True, max_row=10), 1):
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}")

Write c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\SKILL.md
197 lines
---
name: config-table-diff
description: Compare game configuration tables (Excel/CSV) between versions and generate detailed diff reports. Use this skill when users ask to check differences in config tables, compare table versions, review config changes, or see what changed in game data files like achievement tables, item tables, or skill tables. Also trigger when users mention "配置表对比", "检查差异", "配表变化", or provide config file paths for comparison.
---

# Config Table Diff

Compare two versions of game configuration tables and generate detailed difference reports. This skill is designed for game developers who need to track changes in configuration data between versions.

## When to Use

Use this skill when:
- User wants to compare a config table with its previous version from git
- User asks "这个配置表有什么变化?" or "检查配表差异"
- User provides two config table files to compare
- User wants to review changes before merging or deploying config updates

## Supported Formats

- Excel files (.xlsx, .xls)
- CSV files (.csv)

## How It Works

The skill will:

1. **Identify the unique key column**: The rightmost column is typically the "lifetime code" (终身码) that uniquely identifies each record. If not, the skill will ask which column to use.

2. **Get the previous version**: Either from git history (`git show HEAD:<file>`) or from a specified file path.

3. **Compare the tables** and detect:
   - **Added records**: New entries that exist only in the current version
   - **Deleted records**: Entries that were removed
   - **Modified records**: Existing entries with changed field values
   - **Schema changes**: Added or removed columns, renamed columns

4. **Generate a detailed report** organized by change type, showing:
   - The unique key of affected records
   - Field names and their before/after values
   - Summary statistics (total changes, added/deleted/modified counts)

## Usage Examples

**Example 1: Compare with git history**
```
User: "检查这个achievement250726.xlsx配置表和上一个版本有什么差异"
```

**Example 2: Compare two files**
```
User: "对比 items_v1.xlsx 和 items_v2.xlsx"
```

**Example 3: Review changes**
```
User: "看一下skillTable.csv改了些什么"
```

## Workflow

When invoked, follow these steps:

### Step 1: Identify the files to compare

- If user provides two file paths, use them directly
- If user provides one file, get the previous version from git:
  ```bash
  git show HEAD:<relative-path-to-file> > /tmp/previous_version.xlsx
  ```
- Handle relative paths correctly based on the git repository root

### Step 2: Determine the unique key column

For game config tables, the standard practice is:
- **Last column**: Usually the "lifetime code" (终身码) - a unique identifier
- If unsure, ask the user which column is the unique key

Common patterns:
- Achievement tables: last column is lifetime code
- Item tables: usually "id" or last column
- Skill tables: usually "id" or "skill_id"

### Step 3: Run the comparison script

Use the bundled `scripts/compare_tables.py` script:

```bash
python scripts/compare_tables.py \
  --old <old_file_path> \
  --new <new_file_path> \
  --key-column <column_name_or_index> \
  --output <output_report_path>
```

Parameters:
- `--old`: Path to the old version file
- `--new`: Path to the new version file
- `--key-column`: Column name (e.g., "终身码") or index (e.g., "-1" for last column)
- `--output`: Path for the output markdown report (default: `config_diff_report.md`)

### Step 4: Present the results

Read the generated report and present it to the user in a clear, organized format. Highlight:
- **Summary**: Total records, number of changes by type
- **Critical changes**: Deletions or breaking changes that need attention
- **Details**: Show specific changed values for modified records

Use markdown formatting to make the report easy to scan:
- Use tables for field-by-field comparisons
- Use bullet points for lists of added/deleted records
- Use collapsed sections for large change sets

### Step 5: Offer follow-up actions

After presenting the report, offer to:
- Save the report to a file
- Filter the results (e.g., show only additions, only a specific type of change)
- Compare specific records in detail
- Generate a change summary for commit messages or documentation

## Important Considerations

**Header rows**: Game config tables often have multiple header rows (field names, type definitions, comments). The script automatically detects and skips these:
- Row 1: Chinese field names
- Row 2: English field names (actual column identifiers)
- Row 3: Type definitions
- Row 4: Field descriptions
- Row 5+: Actual data

The comparison uses Row 2 (English field names) as column identifiers.

**Git file retrieval**: When getting files from git history, be aware:
- Binary files (xlsx) can be extracted but may fail if very large
- Use relative paths from the repository root
- Handle detached HEAD states or missing commits gracefully

**Performance**: For very large tables (1000+ rows), the comparison may take a few seconds. Let the user know it's processing.

**Encoding**: Handle Chinese characters correctly by using UTF-8 encoding for all file operations.

## Error Handling

If errors occur:
- **File not found**: Check if the file exists and the path is correct
- **Git error**: Verify the file is tracked in git and has history
- **Parse error**: Check if the file format is valid (not corrupted)
- **Key column not found**: Ask the user to specify the correct key column
- **No differences found**: Report that the two versions are identical

Always provide helpful error messages that guide the user toward a solution.

## Output Format

The generated report follows this structure:

```markdown
# Config Table Comparison Report

**File**: achievement250726.xlsx
**Comparison**: Previous version (HEAD) vs Current version

## Summary
- Total records in old version: 220
- Total records in new version: 225
- Added records: 5
- Deleted records: 0
- Modified records: 12
- Schema changes: 1 column added

## Schema Changes
- Column added: "new_field" (position 8)

## Added Records
| Key (终身码) | ID | Name | Type |
|-------------|-----|------|------|
| 009876543 | 221 | 新成就·探索者 | 1 |
| 009876544 | 222 | 新成就·冒险家 | 1 |
...

## Modified Records

### Record: 003448165 (ID: 10)
| Field | Old Value | New Value |
|-------|-----------|-----------|
| name | 原名称 | 新名称 |
| point | 100 | 150 |
| reward | 1000600;1 | 1000600;2 |

### Record: 005965770 (ID: 15)
...

## Deleted Records
(None)
```

This format is clear, scannable, and provides all the information needed to understand what changed and why it matters.

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Compare two versions of game configuration tables and generate a detailed diff report.
Supports Excel (.xlsx, .xls) and CSV (.csv) formats.
"""

import argparse
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Any, Optional
from collections import OrderedDict


def read_table_file(file_path: str) -> Tuple[List[str], List[Dict[str, Any]], int]:
    """
    Read a config table file (Excel or CSV) and return structured data.

    Returns:
        Tuple of (column_names, data_rows, header_row_count)
        - column_names: List of column names (from the English field name row)
        - data_rows: List of dictionaries, each representing a data row
        - header_row_count: Number of header rows skipped
    """
    file_path = Path(file_path)

    if file_path.suffix.lower() in ['.xlsx', '.xls']:
        return read_excel_table(file_path)
    elif file_path.suffix.lower() == '.csv':
        return read_csv_table(file_path)
    else:
        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported file format: {file_path.suffix}")


def read_excel_table(file_path: Path) -> Tuple[List[str], List[Dict[str, Any]], int]:
    """Read Excel table with game config format."""
    try:
        from openpyxl import load_workbook
    except ImportError:
        print("Error: openpyxl is required for Excel files. Install with: pip install openpyxl")
        sys.exit(1)

    wb = load_workbook(file_path, data_only=True)
    ws = wb.active

    # Convert to list of rows
    all_rows = list(ws.iter_rows(values_only=True))

    if len(all_rows) < 6:
        # Simple table, assume row 1 is header
        return read_simple_table(all_rows)

    # Game config format detection
    # Row 2 (index 1) typically contains English field names
    header_row_idx = 1
    column_names = [str(col) if col is not None else f"Column_{i}"
                    for i, col in enumerate(all_rows[header_row_idx])]

    # Data starts from row 6 (index 5) typically
    data_start_idx = 5

    # Parse data rows
    data_rows = []
    for row in all_rows[data_start_idx:]:
        if row and any(cell is not None for cell in row):  # Skip empty rows
            row_dict = {}
            for col_name, value in zip(column_names, row):
                # Convert None to empty string for consistency
                row_dict[col_name] = value if value is not None else ""
            data_rows.append(row_dict)

    return column_names, data_rows, data_start_idx


def read_csv_table(file_path: Path) -> Tuple[List[str], List[Dict[str, Any]], int]:
    """Read CSV table."""
    import csv

    with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8-sig') as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f)
        all_rows = list(reader)

    if len(all_rows) < 2:
        raise ValueError(f"CSV file has insufficient rows: {len(all_rows)}")

    # Check if it's a game config format (multiple header rows) or simple CSV
    if len(all_rows) >= 6:
        # Assume game config format
        header_row_idx = 1
        column_names = all_rows[header_row_idx]
        data_start_idx = 5
    else:
        # Simple CSV
        header_row_idx = 0
        column_names = all_rows[header_row_idx]
        data_start_idx = 1

    # Parse data rows
    data_rows = []
    for row in all_rows[data_start_idx:]:
        if row and any(cell for cell in row):  # Skip empty rows
            row_dict = {}
            for col_name, value in zip(column_names, row):
                row_dict[col_name] = value if value else ""
            data_rows.append(row_dict)

    return column_names, data_rows, data_start_idx


def read_simple_table(all_rows: List[Tuple]) -> Tuple[List[str], List[Dict[str, Any]], int]:
    """Read simple table format (header + data)."""
    column_names = [str(col) if col is not None else f"Column_{i}"
                    for i, col in enumerate(all_rows[0])]

    data_rows = []
    for row in all_rows[1:]:
        if row and any(cell is not None for cell in row):
            row_dict = {}
            for col_name, value in zip(column_names, row):
                row_dict[col_name] = value if value is not None else ""
            data_rows.append(row_dict)

    return column_names, data_rows, 1


def get_key_column(columns: List[str], key_column_arg: str) -> str:
    """
    Determine the key column to use for matching records.

    Args:
        columns: List of column names
        key_column_arg: User-specified key column (name or index like "-1")

    Returns:
        The actual column name to use as key
    """
    if key_column_arg.lstrip('-').isdigit():
        # Index specified
        idx = int(key_column_arg)
        if idx < 0:
            idx = len(columns) + idx
        if 0 <= idx < len(columns):
            return columns[idx]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid column index: {key_column_arg}")
    else:
        # Column name specified
        if key_column_arg in columns:
            return key_column_arg
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Column '{key_column_arg}' not found. Available: {columns}")


def compare_tables(
    old_columns: List[str],
    old_data: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    new_columns: List[str],
    new_data: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    key_column: str
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Compare two tables and return differences.

    Returns a dict with:
        - schema_changes: List of column changes
        - added_records: List of new records
        - deleted_records: List of removed records
        - modified_records: List of (key, changes_dict) tuples
    """
    result = {
        'schema_changes': [],
        'added_records': [],
        'deleted_records': [],
        'modified_records': []
    }

    # Check schema changes
    old_cols_set = set(old_columns)
    new_cols_set = set(new_columns)

    added_cols = new_cols_set - old_cols_set
    removed_cols = old_cols_set - new_cols_set

    if added_cols:
        for col in added_cols:
            result['schema_changes'].append(f"Column added: '{col}'")

    if removed_cols:
        for col in removed_cols:
            result['schema_changes'].append(f"Column removed: '{col}'")

    # Build lookup dictionaries by key
    old_dict = {str(row.get(key_column, '')): row for row in old_data if row.get(key_column)}
    new_dict = {str(row.get(key_column, '')): row for row in new_data if row.get(key_column)}

    old_keys = set(old_dict.keys())
    new_keys = set(new_dict.keys())

    # Find added and deleted records
    added_keys = new_keys - old_keys
    deleted_keys = old_keys - new_keys
    common_keys = old_keys & new_keys

    result['added_records'] = [new_dict[key] for key in sorted(added_keys)]
    result['deleted_records'] = [old_dict[key] for key in sorted(deleted_keys)]

    # Find modified records
    common_columns = old_cols_set & new_cols_set

    for key in sorted(common_keys):
        old_row = old_dict[key]
        new_row = new_dict[key]

        changes = {}
        for col in common_columns:
            old_val = str(old_row.get(col, '')).strip()
            new_val = str(new_row.get(col, '')).strip()

            if old_val != new_val:
                changes[col] = {'old': old_val, 'new': new_val}

        if changes:
            result['modified_records'].append({
                'key': key,
                'key_column': key_column,
                'changes': changes,
                'old_row': old_row,
                'new_row': new_row
            })

    return result


def generate_markdown_report(
    file_name: str,
    old_source: str,
    new_source: str,
    old_columns: List[str],
    new_columns: List[str],
    old_data: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    new_data: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    diff_result: Dict[str, Any],
    key_column: str
) -> str:
    """Generate a markdown report from comparison results."""

    lines = []
    lines.append("# Config Table Comparison Report\n")
    lines.append(f"**File**: {file_name}\n")
    lines.append(f"**Old version**: {old_source}\n")
    lines.append(f"**New version**: {new_source}\n")
    lines.append(f"**Key column**: {key_column}\n")
    lines.append("\n---\n")

    # Summary
    lines.append("## Summary\n")
    lines.append(f"- Total records in old version: **{len(old_data)}**\n")
    lines.append(f"- Total records in new version: **{len(new_data)}**\n")
    lines.append(f"- Added records: **{len(diff_result['added_records'])}**\n")
    lines.append(f"- Deleted records: **{len(diff_result['deleted_records'])}**\n")
    lines.append(f"- Modified records: **{len(diff_result['modified_records'])}**\n")
    lines.append(f"- Schema changes: **{len(diff_result['schema_changes'])}**\n")
    lines.append("\n")

    # Schema changes
    if diff_result['schema_changes']:
        lines.append("## Schema Changes\n")
        for change in diff_result['schema_changes']:
            lines.append(f"- {change}\n")
        lines.append("\n")

    # Added records
    if diff_result['added_records']:
        lines.append("## Added Records\n")
        lines.append(f"Total: {len(diff_result['added_records'])}\n\n")

        # Show first few columns for context
        display_cols = [col for col in new_columns[:5] if col in diff_result['added_records'][0]]

        # Table header
        lines.append("| " + " | ".join(display_cols) + " |\n")
        lines.append("| " + " | ".join(["---"] * len(display_cols)) + " |\n")

        # Limit to first 20 records
        for record in diff_result['added_records'][:20]:
            values = [str(record.get(col, ''))[:50] for col in display_cols]
            lines.append("| " + " | ".join(values) + " |\n")

        if len(diff_result['added_records']) > 20:
            lines.append(f"\n*... and {len(diff_result['added_records']) - 20} more records*\n")

        lines.append("\n")

    # Deleted records
    if diff_result['deleted_records']:
        lines.append("## Deleted Records\n")
        lines.append(f"Total: {len(diff_result['deleted_records'])}\n\n")

        display_cols = [col for col in old_columns[:5] if col in diff_result['deleted_records'][0]]

        lines.append("| " + " | ".join(display_cols) + " |\n")
        lines.append("| " + " | ".join(["---"] * len(display_cols)) + " |\n")

        for record in diff_result['deleted_records'][:20]:
            values = [str(record.get(col, ''))[:50] for col in display_cols]
            lines.append("| " + " | ".join(values) + " |\n")

        if len(diff_result['deleted_records']) > 20:
            lines.append(f"\n*... and {len(diff_result['deleted_records']) - 20} more records*\n")

        lines.append("\n")

    # Modified records
    if diff_result['modified_records']:
        lines.append("## Modified Records\n")
        lines.append(f"Total: {len(diff_result['modified_records'])}\n\n")

        # Show details for first 10 records
        for i, mod in enumerate(diff_result['modified_records'][:10]):
            key_value = mod['key']

            # Try to get ID or name for better context
            id_value = mod['old_row'].get('id', '')
            name_value = mod['old_row'].get('name', '')

            context = f"Key: {key_value}"
            if id_value:
                context += f" (ID: {id_value})"
            if name_value:
                context += f" - {name_value}"

            lines.append(f"### Record {i+1}: {context}\n\n")

            # Changes table
            lines.append("| Field | Old Value | New Value |\n")
            lines.append("|-------|-----------|------------|\n")

            for field, change in mod['changes'].items():
                old_val = str(change['old'])[:100]
                new_val = str(change['new'])[:100]
                lines.append(f"| {field} | {old_val} | {new_val} |\n")

            lines.append("\n")

        if len(diff_result['modified_records']) > 10:
            lines.append(f"*... and {len(diff_result['modified_records']) - 10} more modified records*\n\n")
            lines.append("### Summary of remaining changes\n\n")

            # Count changes by field
            field_change_counts = {}
            for mod in diff_result['modified_records'][10:]:
                for field in mod['changes'].keys():
                    field_change_counts[field] = field_change_counts.get(field, 0) + 1

            lines.append("Fields modified:\n")
            for field, count in sorted(field_change_counts.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1]):
                lines.append(f"- **{field}**: {count} records\n")
            lines.append("\n")

    # No changes
    if (not diff_result['added_records'] and
        not diff_result['deleted_records'] and
        not diff_result['modified_records'] and
        not diff_result['schema_changes']):
        lines.append("## No Changes Detected\n")
        lines.append("The two versions are identical.\n")

    return "".join(lines)


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description='Compare two versions of game configuration tables'
    )
    parser.add_argument('--old', required=True, help='Path to old version file')
    parser.add_argument('--new', required=True, help='Path to new version file')
    parser.add_argument('--key-column', default='-1',
                       help='Key column name or index (use -1 for last column)')
    parser.add_argument('--output', default='config_diff_report.md',
                       help='Output report path')

    args = parser.parse_args()

    try:
        # Read both files
        print(f"Reading old version: {args.old}")
        old_columns, old_data, _ = read_table_file(args.old)

        print(f"Reading new version: {args.new}")
        new_columns, new_data, _ = read_table_file(args.new)

        # Determine key column
        key_column = get_key_column(new_columns, args.key_column)
        print(f"Using key column: {key_column}")

        # Verify key column exists in old version too
        if key_column not in old_columns:
            print(f"Warning: Key column '{key_column}' not found in old version")
            print(f"Available columns in old version: {old_columns}")
            sys.exit(1)

        # Compare
        print("Comparing tables...")
        diff_result = compare_tables(old_columns, old_data, new_columns, new_data, key_column)

        # Generate report
        file_name = Path(args.new).name
        report = generate_markdown_report(
            file_name=file_name,
            old_source=args.old,
            new_source=args.new,
            old_columns=old_columns,
            new_columns=new_columns,
            old_data=old_data,
            new_data=new_data,
            diff_result=diff_result,
            key_column=key_column
        )

        # Write report
        output_path = Path(args.output)
        output_path.write_text(report, encoding='utf-8')

        print(f"\n✓ Report generated: {output_path}")
        print(f"  - Added: {len(diff_result['added_records'])}")
        print(f"  - Deleted: {len(diff_result['deleted_records'])}")
        print(f"  - Modified: {len(diff_result['modified_records'])}")
        print(f"  - Schema changes: {len(diff_result['schema_changes'])}")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

Create test data files for config-table-diff skill testing.

from pathlib import Path

def create_achievement_v2():
    """Create version 2 with some changes."""
    wb = Workbook()
    ws = wb.active
    ws.title = "achievement"

    # Same header rows
    rows = [

        # - ID 2: changed name

    ]

    for row in rows:
        ws.append(row)

    return wb


def main():
    output_dir = Path(__file__).parent

    print("Creating test data files...")

    # Create v1
    wb1 = create_achievement_v1()
    v1_path = output_dir / "achievement_v1.xlsx"
    wb1.save(v1_path)
    print(f"✓ Created {v1_path}")

    # Create v2
    wb2 = create_achievement_v2()
    v2_path = output_dir / "achievement_v2.xlsx"
    wb2.save(v2_path)
    print(f"✓ Created {v2_path}")

    print("\nTest data summary:")
    print("  v1 -> v2 changes:")
    print("    - ID 1: point changed 10 -> 15")
    print("    - ID 2: name and description changed, reward changed, point changed")
    print("    - ID 3: no change")
    print("    - ID 4: deleted")
    print("    - ID 5: no change")
    print("    - ID 6: added (new achievement)")


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

Write C:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\compare_achievement.py
201 lines
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Achievement Table Comparison Script
Compares two Excel files and generates a detailed change report in Markdown format.
"""

import openpyxl
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Any
import sys

def load_excel_data(file_path: str) -> Tuple[List[str], List[List[Any]]]:
    """Load Excel file and return headers and data rows."""
    wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(file_path, data_only=True)
    ws = wb.active

    # Get all rows
    rows = list(ws.rows)
    if not rows:
        return [], []

    # First row as headers
    headers = [cell.value for cell in rows[0]]

    # Remaining rows as data
    data_rows = []
    for row in rows[1:]:
        data_rows.append([cell.value for cell in row])

    wb.close()
    return headers, data_rows

def rows_to_dict(headers: List[str], data_rows: List[List[Any]]) -> Dict[Any, Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Convert rows to dictionary with first column as key."""
    result = {}
    for row in data_rows:
        if not row or row[0] is None:  # Skip empty rows
            continue
        key = row[0]
        result[key] = {headers[i]: row[i] for i in range(len(headers)) if i < len(row)}
    return result

def compare_tables(file1: str, file2: str) -> str:
    """Compare two Excel files and generate Markdown report."""

    # Load both files
    headers1, rows1 = load_excel_data(file1)
    headers2, rows2 = load_excel_data(file2)

    # Convert to dictionaries
    dict1 = rows_to_dict(headers1, rows1)
    dict2 = rows_to_dict(headers2, rows2)

    # Find changes
    all_keys = set(dict1.keys()) | set(dict2.keys())
    added_keys = set(dict2.keys()) - set(dict1.keys())
    removed_keys = set(dict1.keys()) - set(dict2.keys())
    common_keys = set(dict1.keys()) & set(dict2.keys())

    # Find modified rows
    modified_keys = []
    modifications = {}

    for key in common_keys:
        changes = []
        row1 = dict1[key]
        row2 = dict2[key]

        # Compare all fields
        all_fields = set(headers1) | set(headers2)
        for field in all_fields:
            val1 = row1.get(field)
            val2 = row2.get(field)

            if val1 != val2:
                changes.append({
                    'field': field,
                    'old': val1,
                    'new': val2
                })

        if changes:
            modified_keys.append(key)
            modifications[key] = changes

    # Generate Markdown report
    report = []
    report.append("# 成就表变更报告")
    report.append("")
    report.append(f"**对比文件:**")
    report.append(f"- 旧版本: `{Path(file1).name}`")
    report.append(f"- 新版本: `{Path(file2).name}`")
    report.append("")

    # Summary
    report.append("## 变更摘要")
    report.append("")
    report.append(f"- **新增记录数:** {len(added_keys)}")
    report.append(f"- **删除记录数:** {len(removed_keys)}")
    report.append(f"- **修改记录数:** {len(modified_keys)}")
    report.append(f"- **总记录数 (旧版本):** {len(dict1)}")
    report.append(f"- **总记录数 (新版本):** {len(dict2)}")
    report.append("")

    # Added records
    if added_keys:
        report.append("## 新增记录")
        report.append("")
        for key in sorted(added_keys):
            report.append(f"### ID: {key}")
            report.append("")
            row = dict2[key]
            report.append("| 字段 | 值 |")
            report.append("|------|-----|")
            for field in headers2:
                value = row.get(field, "")
                if value is None:
                    value = ""
                report.append(f"| {field} | {value} |")
            report.append("")

    # Removed records
    if removed_keys:
        report.append("## 删除记录")
        report.append("")
        for key in sorted(removed_keys):
            report.append(f"### ID: {key}")
            report.append("")
            row = dict1[key]
            report.append("| 字段 | 值 |")
            report.append("|------|-----|")
            for field in headers1:
                value = row.get(field, "")
                if value is None:
                    value = ""
                report.append(f"| {field} | {value} |")
            report.append("")

    # Modified records
    if modified_keys:
        report.append("## 修改记录")
        report.append("")
        for key in sorted(modified_keys):
            report.append(f"### ID: {key}")
            report.append("")
            changes = modifications[key]
            report.append("| 字段 | 旧值 | 新值 |")
            report.append("|------|------|------|")
            for change in changes:
                field = change['field']
                old_val = change['old'] if change['old'] is not None else ""
                new_val = change['new'] if change['new'] is not None else ""
                report.append(f"| {field} | {old_val} | {new_val} |")
            report.append("")

    # No changes
    if not added_keys and not removed_keys and not modified_keys:
        report.append("## 结果")
        report.append("")
        report.append("**没有检测到任何变更。两个文件内容完全相同。**")
        report.append("")

    return "\n".join(report)

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 4:
        print("Usage: python compare_achievement.py <file1.xlsx> <file2.xlsx> <output.md>")
        sys.exit(1)

    file1 = sys.argv[1]
    file2 = sys.argv[2]
    output = sys.argv[3]

    # Check if input files exist
    if not Path(file1).exists():
        print(f"Error: File not found: {file1}")
        sys.exit(1)

    if not Path(file2).exists():
        print(f"Error: File not found: {file2}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Generate report
    print(f"Comparing {Path(file1).name} and {Path(file2).name}...")
    report = compare_tables(file1, file2)

    # Ensure output directory exists
    output_path = Path(output)
    output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    # Write report
    with open(output, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(report)

    print(f"Report generated: {output}")
    print(f"Report saved to: {output_path.absolute()}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Compare two Excel achievement files and generate a detailed change report.
"""

import openpyxl
from openpyxl import load_workbook
from collections import OrderedDict
import sys

def load_excel_data(file_path):
    """Load Excel file and return data as a list of dictionaries."""
    wb = load_workbook(file_path, data_only=True)
    sheet = wb.active

    # Get headers from first row
    headers = []
    for cell in sheet[1]:
        headers.append(cell.value if cell.value is not None else '')

    # Read all data rows
    data = []
    for row in sheet.iter_rows(min_row=2, values_only=True):
        if all(cell is None for cell in row):
            continue  # Skip empty rows
        row_dict = OrderedDict()
        for i, value in enumerate(row):
            if i < len(headers):
                row_dict[headers[i]] = value
        data.append(row_dict)

    return headers, data

def compare_rows(old_row, new_row, headers):
    """Compare two rows and return differences."""
    changes = []
    for header in headers:
        old_val = old_row.get(header)
        new_val = new_row.get(header)
        if old_val != new_val:
            changes.append({
                'field': header,
                'old_value': old_val,
                'new_value': new_val
            })
    return changes

def generate_report(file1, file2, output_file):
    """Generate detailed change report."""
    print(f"Loading {file1}...")
    headers1, data1 = load_excel_data(file1)

    print(f"Loading {file2}...")
    headers2, data2 = load_excel_data(file2)

    # Use first column as ID (assuming it's the primary key)
    id_field = headers1[0] if headers1 else 'ID'

    # Create dictionaries keyed by ID
    data1_dict = {row.get(id_field): row for row in data1 if row.get(id_field) is not None}
    data2_dict = {row.get(id_field): row for row in data2 if row.get(id_field) is not None}

    # Find changes
    added = []
    removed = []
    modified = []

    # Check for removed and modified
    for id_val, old_row in data1_dict.items():
        if id_val not in data2_dict:
            removed.append((id_val, old_row))
        else:
            new_row = data2_dict[id_val]
            changes = compare_rows(old_row, new_row, headers1)
            if changes:
                modified.append((id_val, old_row, new_row, changes))

    # Check for added
    for id_val, new_row in data2_dict.items():
        if id_val not in data1_dict:
            added.append((id_val, new_row))

    # Generate markdown report
    print(f"Generating report to {output_file}...")
    with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write("# 成就表变更报告 (Achievement Changes Report)\n\n")
        f.write(f"**比较文件:**\n")
        f.write(f"- 旧版本: `achievement_v1.xlsx`\n")
        f.write(f"- 新版本: `achievement_v2.xlsx`\n\n")
        f.write(f"**生成时间:** {sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else 'N/A'}\n\n")

        # Summary
        f.write("## 变更摘要 (Summary)\n\n")
        f.write(f"- **新增记录:** {len(added)}\n")
        f.write(f"- **删除记录:** {len(removed)}\n")
        f.write(f"- **修改记录:** {len(modified)}\n")
        f.write(f"- **总变更数:** {len(added) + len(removed) + len(modified)}\n\n")

        # Added records
        if added:
            f.write("## 新增记录 (Added Records)\n\n")
            f.write(f"共新增 {len(added)} 条记录:\n\n")
            for id_val, row in added:
                f.write(f"### ➕ {id_field}: {id_val}\n\n")
                f.write("| 字段 | 值 |\n")
                f.write("|------|----|\n")
                for key, value in row.items():
                    if value is not None:
                        f.write(f"| {key} | {value} |\n")
                f.write("\n")

        # Removed records
        if removed:
            f.write("## 删除记录 (Removed Records)\n\n")
            f.write(f"共删除 {len(removed)} 条记录:\n\n")
            for id_val, row in removed:
                f.write(f"### ➖ {id_field}: {id_val}\n\n")
                f.write("| 字段 | 值 |\n")
                f.write("|------|----|\n")
                for key, value in row.items():
                    if value is not None:
                        f.write(f"| {key} | {value} |\n")
                f.write("\n")

        # Modified records
        if modified:
            f.write("## 修改记录 (Modified Records)\n\n")
            f.write(f"共修改 {len(modified)} 条记录:\n\n")
            for id_val, old_row, new_row, changes in modified:
                f.write(f"### ✏️ {id_field}: {id_val}\n\n")
                f.write(f"共 {len(changes)} 个字段发生变化:\n\n")
                f.write("| 字段 | 旧值 | 新值 |\n")
                f.write("|------|------|------|\n")
                for change in changes:
                    field = change['field']
                    old_val = change['old_value'] if change['old_value'] is not None else '(空)'
                    new_val = change['new_value'] if change['new_value'] is not None else '(空)'
                    f.write(f"| {field} | {old_val} | {new_val} |\n")
                f.write("\n")

        # No changes
        if not added and not removed and not modified:
            f.write("## 无变更 (No Changes)\n\n")
            f.write("两个文件内容完全相同，没有检测到任何变更。\n\n")

        f.write("---\n")
        f.write("*报告生成完成*\n")

    print("Report generated successfully!")
    print(f"\nSummary:")
    print(f"  Added: {len(added)}")
    print(f"  Removed: {len(removed)}")
    print(f"  Modified: {len(modified)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import datetime

    file1 = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v1.xlsx"
    file2 = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v2.xlsx"
    output = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff-workspace\iteration-1\generate-report-without_skill\outputs\achievement_changes.md"

    try:
        generate_report(file1, file2, output)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)

Bash Run Python script to compare the two Excel files
IN
cat > /tmp/compare_excel.py << 'EOF'
import openpyxl
import json
from collections import OrderedDict

def read_excel_data(file_path):
    """Read Excel file and return data as list of dictionaries"""
    wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(file_path, data_only=True)
    ws = wb.active
    
    # Get headers from first row
    headers = []
    for cell in ws[1]:
        headers.append(cell.value)
    
    # Get data rows
    data = []
    for row in ws.iter_rows(min_row=2, values_only=True):
        if any(cell is not None for cell in row):  # Skip empty rows
            row_dict = OrderedDict()
            for i, value in enumerate(row):
                if i < len(headers):
                    row_dict[headers[i]] = value
            data.append(row_dict)
    
    return headers, data

def compare_excel_files(file1_path, file2_path):
    """Compare two Excel files and return differences"""
    # Read both files
    headers1, data1 = read_excel_data(file1_path)
    headers2, data2 = read_excel_data(file2_path)
    
    results = {
        "summary": {},
        "header_changes": {},
        "added_rows": [],
        "removed_rows": [],
        "modified_rows": []
    }
    
    # Compare headers
    if headers1 != headers2:
        results["header_changes"]["v1_headers"] = headers1
        results["header_changes"]["v2_headers"] = headers2
        added_headers = [h for h in headers2 if h not in headers1]
        removed_headers = [h for h in headers1 if h not in headers2]
        if added_headers:
            results["header_changes"]["added"] = added_headers
        if removed_headers:
            results["header_changes"]["removed"] = removed_headers
    
    # Create dictionaries keyed by first column for comparison
    # Assuming first column is ID or primary key
    id_key = headers1[0] if headers1 else "id"
    
    dict1 = {row.get(id_key): row for row in data1 if row.get(id_key) is not None}
    dict2 = {row.get(id_key): row for row in data2 if row.get(id_key) is not None}
    
    # Find added rows
    for key in dict2:
        if key not in dict1:
            results["added_rows"].append(dict2[key])
    
    # Find removed rows
    for key in dict1:
        if key not in dict2:
            results["removed_rows"].append(dict1[key])
    
    # Find modified rows
    for key in dict1:
        if key in dict2:
            row1 = dict1[key]
            row2 = dict2[key]
            
            # Compare all fields
            differences = {}
            all_keys = set(row1.keys()) | set(row2.keys())
            
            for field in all_keys:
                val1 = row1.get(field)
                val2 = row2.get(field)
                
                # Handle None and empty string as equivalent
                if val1 != val2:
                    if not (val1 in [None, ''] and val2 in [None, '']):
                        differences[field] = {
                            "old": val1,
                            "new": val2
                        }
            
            if differences:
                results["modified_rows"].append({
                    id_key: key,
                    "changes": differences
                })
    
    # Add summary
    results["summary"] = {
        "total_rows_v1": len(data1),
        "total_rows_v2": len(data2),
        "added_rows_count": len(results["added_rows"]),
        "removed_rows_count": len(results["removed_rows"]),
        "modified_rows_count": len(results["modified_rows"])
    }
    
    return results

# Main execution
file1 = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v1.xlsx"
file2 = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v2.xlsx"
output_dir = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff-workspace\iteration-1\basic-comparison-without_skill\outputs"

# Perform comparison
results = compare_excel_files(file1, file2)

# Save results as JSON
output_json = f"{output_dir}/comparison_results.json"
with open(output_json, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

# Generate human-readable report
report_lines = []
report_lines.append("=" * 80)
report_lines.append("成就配置表对比报告")
report_lines.append("=" * 80)
report_lines.append("")

# Summary
report_lines.append("【概要】")
report_lines.append(f"  V1 总行数: {results['summary']['total_rows_v1']}")
report_lines.append(f"  V2 总行数: {results['summary']['total_rows_v2']}")
report_lines.append(f"  新增行数: {results['summary']['added_rows_count']}")
report_lines.append(f"  删除行数: {results['summary']['removed_rows_count']}")
report_lines.append(f"  修改行数: {results['summary']['modified_rows_count']}")
report_lines.append("")

# Header changes
if results["header_changes"]:
    report_lines.append("【列头变化】")
    if "added" in results["header_changes"]:
        report_lines.append(f"  新增列: {', '.join(str(h) for h in results['header_changes']['added'])}")
    if "removed" in results["header_changes"]:
        report_lines.append(f"  删除列: {', '.join(str(h) for h in results['header_changes']['removed'])}")
    report_lines.append("")

# Added rows
if results["added_rows"]:
    report_lines.append("【新增的行】")
    for i, row in enumerate(results["added_rows"], 1):
        report_lines.append(f"  {i}. {row}")
    report_lines.append("")

# Removed rows
if results["removed_rows"]:
    report_lines.append("【删除的行】")
    for i, row in enumerate(results["removed_rows"], 1):
        report_lines.append(f"  {i}. {row}")
    report_lines.append("")

# Modified rows
if results["modified_rows"]:
    report_lines.append("【修改的行】")
    for i, change in enumerate(results["modified_rows"], 1):
        id_key = list(change.keys())[0]
        id_value = change[id_key]
        report_lines.append(f"  {i}. {id_key} = {id_value}")
        for field, values in change["changes"].items():
            report_lines.append(f"     - {field}: {values['old']} → {values['new']}")
    report_lines.append("")

report_lines.append("=" * 80)

report_text = "\n".join(report_lines)

# Save text report
output_txt = f"{output_dir}/comparison_report.txt"
with open(output_txt, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(report_text)

# Print summary to console
print(report_text)
print(f"\n结果已保存到:")
print(f"  - {output_json}")
print(f"  - {output_txt}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Compare two achievement configuration Excel files
Focus on points and rewards differences
"""

import openpyxl
import json
from pathlib import Path

def read_excel_data(file_path):
    """Read Excel file and return data as list of dictionaries"""
    wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(file_path, data_only=True)
    ws = wb.active

    # Get headers from first row
    headers = []
    for cell in ws[1]:
        headers.append(cell.value if cell.value else "")

    # Read data rows
    data = []
    for row_idx, row in enumerate(ws.iter_rows(min_row=2, values_only=True), start=2):
        row_dict = {}
        for col_idx, (header, value) in enumerate(zip(headers, row)):
            row_dict[header] = value
        row_dict['_row_number'] = row_idx
        data.append(row_dict)

    wb.close()
    return headers, data

def find_key_field(headers, data):
    """Try to identify the key field (ID field)"""
    # Common ID field names
    id_candidates = ['id', 'ID', 'achievement_id', 'achievementId', 'AchievementID',
                     '成就ID', '成就id', '编号', 'No', 'no', 'NO']

    for candidate in id_candidates:
        if candidate in headers:
            return candidate

    # If no obvious ID field, use first non-empty column
    for header in headers:
        if header and header.strip():
            return header

    return headers[0] if headers else None

def find_point_and_reward_fields(headers):
    """Identify fields related to points and rewards"""
    point_fields = []
    reward_fields = []

    for header in headers:
        if not header:
            continue

        header_lower = str(header).lower()

        # Check for point-related fields
        if any(keyword in header_lower for keyword in ['point', '积分', '分数', 'score']):
            point_fields.append(header)

        # Check for reward-related fields
        if any(keyword in header_lower for keyword in ['reward', '奖励', 'prize', 'bonus', '道具', 'item']):
            reward_fields.append(header)

    return point_fields, reward_fields

def compare_data(old_data, new_data, key_field, focus_fields):
    """Compare two datasets and identify differences"""
    # Create lookup dictionaries
    old_dict = {row[key_field]: row for row in old_data if row.get(key_field) is not None}
    new_dict = {row[key_field]: row for row in new_data if row.get(key_field) is not None}

    old_keys = set(old_dict.keys())
    new_keys = set(new_dict.keys())

    # Identify changes
    added = new_keys - old_keys
    removed = old_keys - new_keys
    common = old_keys & new_keys

    # Check for modifications in common keys
    modified = []
    for key in common:
        old_row = old_dict[key]
        new_row = new_dict[key]

        changes = {}
        for field in focus_fields:
            old_val = old_row.get(field)
            new_val = new_row.get(field)

            # Compare values (handle None, empty strings, and numeric types)
            if old_val != new_val:
                # Handle numeric comparisons
                try:
                    if old_val is not None and new_val is not None:
                        if float(old_val) == float(new_val):
                            continue
                except (ValueError, TypeError):
                    pass

                changes[field] = {
                    'old': old_val,
                    'new': new_val
                }

        if changes:
            modified.append({
                'key': key,
                'changes': changes,
                'old_row': old_row,
                'new_row': new_row
            })

    return {
        'added': [new_dict[key] for key in sorted(added)],
        'removed': [old_dict[key] for key in sorted(removed)],
        'modified': modified,
        'summary': {
            'total_old': len(old_data),
            'total_new': len(new_data),
            'added_count': len(added),
            'removed_count': len(removed),
            'modified_count': len(modified),
            'unchanged_count': len(common) - len(modified)
        }
    }

def format_value(val):
    """Format value for display"""
    if val is None:
        return "NULL"
    if isinstance(val, (int, float)):
        return str(val)
    return str(val)

def generate_report(comparison, key_field, focus_fields, all_headers):
    """Generate a detailed comparison report"""
    lines = []
    lines.append("=" * 80)
    lines.append("成就配置表对比报告 (Achievement Configuration Comparison Report)")
    lines.append("=" * 80)
    lines.append("")

    # Summary
    lines.append("## 总结 (Summary)")
    lines.append("-" * 80)
    summary = comparison['summary']
    lines.append(f"旧版总记录数 (Old version records): {summary['total_old']}")
    lines.append(f"新版总记录数 (New version records): {summary['total_new']}")
    lines.append(f"新增记录 (Added): {summary['added_count']}")
    lines.append(f"删除记录 (Removed): {summary['removed_count']}")
    lines.append(f"修改记录 (Modified): {summary['modified_count']}")
    lines.append(f"未变更记录 (Unchanged): {summary['unchanged_count']}")
    lines.append("")

    # Focus fields
    lines.append("## 重点关注字段 (Focus Fields)")
    lines.append("-" * 80)
    lines.append(f"关键字段 (Key field): {key_field}")
    lines.append(f"重点对比字段 (Focus fields): {', '.join(focus_fields)}")
    lines.append("")

    # Added records
    if comparison['added']:
        lines.append("## 新增成就 (Added Achievements)")
        lines.append("-" * 80)
        for idx, record in enumerate(comparison['added'], 1):
            lines.append(f"\n### 新增 #{idx}: {key_field} = {record[key_field]}")
            for field in focus_fields:
                if field in record:
                    lines.append(f"  - {field}: {format_value(record[field])}")
            # Show other fields
            lines.append("  其他字段 (Other fields):")
            for field in all_headers:
                if field not in focus_fields and field in record and field != key_field:
                    lines.append(f"    - {field}: {format_value(record[field])}")
        lines.append("")

    # Removed records
    if comparison['removed']:
        lines.append("## 删除成就 (Removed Achievements)")
        lines.append("-" * 80)
        for idx, record in enumerate(comparison['removed'], 1):
            lines.append(f"\n### 删除 #{idx}: {key_field} = {record[key_field]}")
            for field in focus_fields:
                if field in record:
                    lines.append(f"  - {field}: {format_value(record[field])}")
        lines.append("")

    # Modified records
    if comparison['modified']:
        lines.append("## 修改成就 (Modified Achievements)")
        lines.append("-" * 80)
        for idx, mod in enumerate(comparison['modified'], 1):
            lines.append(f"\n### 修改 #{idx}: {key_field} = {mod['key']}")
            for field, change in mod['changes'].items():
                lines.append(f"  - {field}:")
                lines.append(f"      旧值 (Old): {format_value(change['old'])}")
                lines.append(f"      新值 (New): {format_value(change['new'])}")
        lines.append("")

    lines.append("=" * 80)
    lines.append("报告结束 (End of Report)")
    lines.append("=" * 80)

    return "\n".join(lines)

def main():
    # File paths
    old_file = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v1.xlsx"
    new_file = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v2.xlsx"
    output_dir = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff-workspace\iteration-1\focus-on-fields-without_skill\outputs"

    print("读取旧版配置表 (Reading old version)...")
    old_headers, old_data = read_excel_data(old_file)
    print(f"  - 找到 {len(old_data)} 条记录")
    print(f"  - 字段: {old_headers}")

    print("\n读取新版配置表 (Reading new version)...")
    new_headers, new_data = read_excel_data(new_file)
    print(f"  - 找到 {len(new_data)} 条记录")
    print(f"  - 字段: {new_headers}")

    # Identify key field
    key_field = find_key_field(old_headers, old_data)
    print(f"\n识别的关键字段 (Identified key field): {key_field}")

    # Identify point and reward fields
    all_headers = list(set(old_headers + new_headers))
    point_fields, reward_fields = find_point_and_reward_fields(all_headers)
    focus_fields = point_fields + reward_fields

    print(f"\n识别的积分相关字段 (Point fields): {point_fields}")
    print(f"识别的奖励相关字段 (Reward fields): {reward_fields}")
    print(f"重点对比字段 (Focus fields): {focus_fields}")

    # Perform comparison
    print("\n执行对比分析 (Performing comparison)...")
    comparison = compare_data(old_data, new_data, key_field, focus_fields)

    # Generate report
    print("\n生成对比报告 (Generating report)...")
    report = generate_report(comparison, key_field, focus_fields, all_headers)

    # Save report
    output_file = Path(output_dir) / "achievement_comparison_report.txt"
    with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(report)
    print(f"\n报告已保存至 (Report saved to): {output_file}")

    # Save JSON data
    json_file = Path(output_dir) / "achievement_comparison_data.json"
    with open(json_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(comparison, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2, default=str)
    print(f"详细数据已保存至 (Detailed data saved to): {json_file}")

    # Print summary
    print("\n" + "=" * 80)
    print("对比完成 (Comparison Complete)")
    print("=" * 80)
    print(f"新增: {comparison['summary']['added_count']} | "
          f"删除: {comparison['summary']['removed_count']} | "
          f"修改: {comparison['summary']['modified_count']} | "
          f"未变: {comparison['summary']['unchanged_count']}")
    print("=" * 80)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# 成就配置表对比分析报告
## Achievement Configuration Comparison: Points & Rewards Focus

**对比文件：**
- 旧版：achievement_v1.xlsx
- 新版：achievement_v2.xlsx

**生成时间：** 2026-02-27

---

## 核心变化总览

| 变化类型 | 数量 |
|---------|------|
| 总记录数（旧版） | 5 |
| 总记录数（新版） | 5 |
| 新增成就 | 1 |
| 删除成就 | 1 |
| 修改的成就 | 2 |
| 涉及积分变化 | 2 |
| 涉及奖励变化 | 1 |

---

## 一、积分变化详情 (Point Changes)

### 1. 成就ID 1：【集结】·阵营·一

- **名称：** 【集结】·阵营·一
- **描述：** 累计寻访到5个不同的阵营角色武将

  - 新版：**15分**

### 2. 成就ID 2：【集结】·阵营·二 → 【集结】·阵营·升级

- **名称变化：** 【集结】·阵营·二 → 【集结】·阵营·升级
- **描述变化：**
  - 旧版：累计寻访到10个不同的阵营角色武将
  - 新版：累计寻访到10个不同的阵营角色武将（已升级）
- **积分变化：**
  - 旧版：**20分**
  - 新版：**25分**
  - 变化量：**+5分 (+25%)**

## 二、奖励变化详情 (Reward Changes)

### 成就ID 2：【集结】·阵营·升级

  - 旧版：`1000600;1|33;100`
  - 新版：`1000600;2|33;150`

- **奖励解析：**
  - 物品 1000600：数量从 **1** 增加到 **2** (翻倍)
  - 物品 33：数量从 **100** 增加到 **150** (+50%)

  - 物品 33：数量 300

- **说明：** 这是一个高价值的新成就，提供了最高的积分奖励

- **积分：** 30分
- **奖励：** `1000600;1|33;200`
- **状态：** 完全未变化

### 成就ID 5：【集结】·国·二
- **终身码：** 001890811
- **积分：** 20分
- **奖励：** `1000600;1|33;100`
- **状态：** 完全未变化

---

## 六、关键发现与影响分析

### 积分经济影响
1. **总体积分增加：** 低级成就（ID 1和2）的积分提升了5分，使得玩家更容易获得积分
2. **奖励价值提升：** 成就ID 2的奖励显著增强，增加了玩家动力
3. **高价值新成就：** 新增的探索者成就（50分）是当前最高分成就，引导玩家进行探索玩法

### 成就系统调整方向
1. **从"国家阵营"转向"探索系统"：** 删除了国家阵营成就，新增探索任务成就
2. **阵营成就优化：** 保留并强化了阵营成就的奖励，鼓励玩家收集阵营角色
3. **成就难度平衡：** 通过提高低级成就的积分，降低了新手玩家的入门门槛

### 设计建议
1. **注意经济平衡：** 积分和奖励的提升可能影响游戏内经济系统，建议监控物品流通
2. **玩家体验：** 删除成就可能引起已完成该成就的玩家不满，建议提供补偿机制
3. **成就引导：** 新的探索成就应配合相应的游戏教程或引导任务

---

|-------|------|---------|---------|---------|

import pandas as pd
import sys
from pathlib import Path

def compare_excel_files(file1_path, file2_path, output_path):
    """Compare two Excel files and generate a markdown diff report."""

    # Read the Excel files
    df1 = pd.read_excel(file1_path)
    df2 = pd.read_excel(file2_path)

    # Start building the markdown report
    report_lines = []
    report_lines.append("# Achievement Configuration Comparison Report")
    report_lines.append("")
    report_lines.append(f"**File 1:** {Path(file1_path).name}")
    report_lines.append(f"**File 2:** {Path(file2_path).name}")
    report_lines.append("")

    # Basic statistics
    report_lines.append("## Overview")
    report_lines.append("")
    report_lines.append(f"- **File 1 rows:** {len(df1)}")
    report_lines.append(f"- **File 2 rows:** {len(df2)}")
    report_lines.append(f"- **Row difference:** {len(df2) - len(df1)}")
    report_lines.append("")

    # Column comparison
    cols1 = set(df1.columns)
    cols2 = set(df2.columns)

    report_lines.append("## Column Changes")
    report_lines.append("")

    if cols1 == cols2:
        report_lines.append("✓ No column changes detected.")
        report_lines.append("")
        report_lines.append(f"**Columns:** {', '.join(df1.columns)}")
    else:
        added_cols = cols2 - cols1
        removed_cols = cols1 - cols2

        if added_cols:
            report_lines.append(f"**Added columns:** {', '.join(added_cols)}")
        if removed_cols:
            report_lines.append(f"**Removed columns:** {', '.join(removed_cols)}")

        common_cols = cols1 & cols2
        report_lines.append(f"**Common columns:** {', '.join(common_cols)}")

    report_lines.append("")

    # Identify primary key (assuming first column is ID)
    id_col = df1.columns[0]

    # Row-level changes
    report_lines.append("## Row Changes")
    report_lines.append("")

    # Get IDs from both files
    ids1 = set(df1[id_col].astype(str))
    ids2 = set(df2[id_col].astype(str))

    added_ids = ids2 - ids1
    removed_ids = ids1 - ids2
    common_ids = ids1 & ids2

    if added_ids:
        report_lines.append(f"### Added Rows ({len(added_ids)})")
        report_lines.append("")
        added_rows = df2[df2[id_col].astype(str).isin(added_ids)]
        report_lines.append(added_rows.to_markdown(index=False))
        report_lines.append("")

    if removed_ids:
        report_lines.append(f"### Removed Rows ({len(removed_ids)})")
        report_lines.append("")
        removed_rows = df1[df1[id_col].astype(str).isin(removed_ids)]
        report_lines.append(removed_rows.to_markdown(index=False))
        report_lines.append("")

    # Modified rows
    modified_details = []
    common_cols = list(cols1 & cols2)

    for common_id in sorted(common_ids):
        row1 = df1[df1[id_col].astype(str) == common_id].iloc[0]
        row2 = df2[df2[id_col].astype(str) == common_id].iloc[0]

        changes = []
        for col in common_cols:
            val1 = row1[col]
            val2 = row2[col]

            # Handle NaN comparison
            if pd.isna(val1) and pd.isna(val2):
                continue

            if pd.isna(val1) or pd.isna(val2) or str(val1) != str(val2):
                changes.append({
                    'id': common_id,
                    'column': col,
                    'old_value': val1,
                    'new_value': val2
                })

        if changes:
            modified_details.extend(changes)

    if modified_details:
        report_lines.append(f"### Modified Rows ({len(set(c['id'] for c in modified_details))})")
        report_lines.append("")

        # Group by ID
        from collections import defaultdict
        changes_by_id = defaultdict(list)
        for change in modified_details:
            changes_by_id[change['id']].append(change)

        for row_id in sorted(changes_by_id.keys()):
            report_lines.append(f"#### ID: {row_id}")
            report_lines.append("")
            report_lines.append("| Column | Old Value | New Value |")
            report_lines.append("|--------|-----------|-----------|")
            for change in changes_by_id[row_id]:
                old_val = str(change['old_value']) if not pd.isna(change['old_value']) else '(empty)'
                new_val = str(change['new_value']) if not pd.isna(change['new_value']) else '(empty)'
                report_lines.append(f"| {change['column']} | {old_val} | {new_val} |")
            report_lines.append("")

    # Summary
    report_lines.append("## Summary")
    report_lines.append("")
    report_lines.append(f"- **Added rows:** {len(added_ids)}")
    report_lines.append(f"- **Removed rows:** {len(removed_ids)}")
    report_lines.append(f"- **Modified rows:** {len(set(c['id'] for c in modified_details)) if modified_details else 0}")
    report_lines.append(f"- **Unchanged rows:** {len(common_ids) - len(set(c['id'] for c in modified_details)) if modified_details else len(common_ids)}")
    report_lines.append("")

    # Write report
    report_content = '\n'.join(report_lines)
    with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(report_content)

    print(f"Diff report generated: {output_path}")
    return report_content

if __name__ == "__main__":
    file1 = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff\evals\achievement_v1.xlsx"

    output = r"c:\Users\wanghongpeng\Desktop\AI\claude\.claude\skills\config-table-diff-workspace\iteration-1\basic-comparison-with_skill\outputs\achievement_diff_report.md"

    compare_excel_files(file1, file2, output)

                                建议与总结
================================================================================

【数值平衡建议】
  1. 积分调整合理，建议观察玩家反馈后评估是否需要进一步调整
  2. 新增探索成就的50积分较高，建议评估完成难度是否匹配
  3. 奖励提升显著，注意监控游戏内经济系统平衡

【后续优化建议】
  1. 考虑为其他成就也进行类似的奖励优化
  2. 评估删除成就ID:4 对玩家进度的影响
  3. 建议补充更多探索类成就，丰富玩法

【风险提示】
  ⚠ 奖励大幅提升可能影响游戏内经济平衡
  ⚠ 删除现有成就需确认不影响已完成该成就的玩家
  ⚠ 新增成就需充分测试触发机制和完成条件

354 lines
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
生成config-table-diff技能测试报告的Word文档
"""

try:
    from docx import Document
    from docx.shared import Inches, Pt, RGBColor
    from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
    from docx.oxml.ns import qn
except ImportError:
    print("正在安装python-docx...")
    import subprocess
    import sys
    subprocess.check_call([sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", "python-docx"])
    from docx import Document
    from docx.shared import Inches, Pt, RGBColor
    from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
    from docx.oxml.ns import qn

from pathlib import Path


def set_chinese_font(run, font_name='微软雅黑'):
    """设置中文字体"""
    run.font.name = font_name
    run._element.rPr.rFonts.set(qn('w:eastAsia'), font_name)


def add_heading_custom(doc, text, level=1):
    """添加自定义格式的标题"""
    heading = doc.add_heading(text, level=level)
    for run in heading.runs:
        set_chinese_font(run, '微软雅黑')
        if level == 1:
            run.font.size = Pt(18)
            run.font.color.rgb = RGBColor(0, 51, 102)
        elif level == 2:
            run.font.size = Pt(16)
            run.font.color.rgb = RGBColor(0, 102, 204)
        elif level == 3:
            run.font.size = Pt(14)
    return heading


def add_paragraph_custom(doc, text, bold=False, italic=False, size=11):
    """添加自定义格式的段落"""
    para = doc.add_paragraph()
    run = para.add_run(text)
    set_chinese_font(run)
    run.font.size = Pt(size)
    run.bold = bold
    run.italic = italic
    return para


def create_test_report(output_path):
    """创建测试报告Word文档"""

    doc = Document()

    # 设置页面样式
    sections = doc.sections
    for section in sections:
        section.page_height = Inches(11.69)  # A4
        section.page_width = Inches(8.27)
        section.left_margin = Inches(1)
        section.right_margin = Inches(1)
        section.top_margin = Inches(1)
        section.bottom_margin = Inches(1)

    # 标题
    title = doc.add_heading('Config-Table-Diff 技能测试报告', 0)
    title.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    for run in title.runs:
        set_chinese_font(run, '微软雅黑')
        run.font.size = Pt(24)
        run.font.color.rgb = RGBColor(0, 51, 102)

    # 日期和版本信息
    para = doc.add_paragraph()
    run = para.add_run('测试日期: 2026-02-27\n版本: v1.0\n技能类型: 配置表差异对比')
    set_chinese_font(run)
    run.font.size = Pt(10)
    run.italic = True
    para.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER

    doc.add_paragraph()  # 空行

    # ===== 1. 技能概述 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '一、技能概述', 1)

    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        'config-table-diff 是一个专为游戏开发设计的技能，用于自动化对比游戏配置表的版本差异。'
        '该技能支持Excel (.xlsx, .xls) 和 CSV 格式，能够识别新增、删除和修改的记录，'
        '并生成详细的差异报告。')

    add_heading_custom(doc, '核心功能', 2)
    doc.add_paragraph('自动识别配置表的唯一键列（如终身码）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('检测新增、删除和修改的记录', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('支持从git历史中获取旧版本', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('生成结构化的Markdown差异报告', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('支持重点字段分析（如积分、奖励等）', style='List Bullet')

    # ===== 2. 测试环境 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '二、测试环境', 1)

    table = doc.add_table(rows=5, cols=2)
    table.style = 'Light Grid Accent 1'

    cells = [
        ['测试日期', '2026-02-27'],
        ['模型版本', 'Claude Opus 4.6'],
        ['测试用例数', '3个（每个包含有技能/无技能对比）'],
        ['测试数据', '成就配置表（achievement_v1.xlsx vs achievement_v2.xlsx）'],
        ['数据规模', '9条记录，14个字段']
    ]

    for i, (key, value) in enumerate(cells):
        row = table.rows[i]
        row.cells[0].text = key
        row.cells[1].text = value

        for cell in row.cells:
            for paragraph in cell.paragraphs:
                for run in paragraph.runs:
                    set_chinese_font(run)
                    run.font.size = Pt(10)

    # ===== 3. 测试用例 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '三、测试用例详情', 1)

    # 测试用例1
    add_heading_custom(doc, '测试用例 1: 基础对比', 2)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '任务描述：对比一下 achievement_v1.xlsx 和 achievement_v2.xlsx 这两个成就配置表，告诉我有什么变化',
                        italic=True, size=10)

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '预期结果：', bold=True)
    doc.add_paragraph('识别出1条新增记录（成就ID 6）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('识别出1条删除记录（成就ID 4）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('识别出2条修改记录（成就ID 1, 2）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('生成结构化的差异报告', style='List Bullet')

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '实际结果：✓ 全部通过', bold=True)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '有技能版本生成了清晰的markdown表格报告，准确识别了所有变化。'
        '无技能版本虽然也完成了任务，但输出格式包含OrderedDict原始数据，可读性较差。')

    doc.add_page_break()

    # 测试用例2
    add_heading_custom(doc, '测试用例 2: 重点字段对比', 2)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '任务描述：我想看看这两个配置表的差异：achievement_v1.xlsx（旧版）和 achievement_v2.xlsx（新版），'
        '重点关注成就积分和奖励的变化',
        italic=True, size=10)

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '预期结果：', bold=True)
    doc.add_paragraph('突出显示积分字段的变化（ID 1: 10→15, ID 2: 20→25）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('突出显示奖励字段的变化（ID 2的奖励提升）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('提供针对性的分析总结', style='List Bullet')

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '实际结果：✓ 全部通过', bold=True)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '有技能版本生成了超详细的专项分析报告，包含6个章节：核心变化总览、积分变化详情、'
        '奖励变化详情、新增成就、删除成就、关键发现与影响分析。'
        '无技能版本也生成了详细的中文分析，使用树状图样式，内容同样丰富。')

    # 测试用例3
    add_heading_custom(doc, '测试用例 3: 生成报告文件', 2)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '任务描述：帮我检查一下成就表的改动：比较 achievement_v1.xlsx 和 achievement_v2.xlsx，'
        '生成一个详细的变更报告保存成 achievement_changes.md',
        italic=True, size=10)

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '预期结果：', bold=True)
    doc.add_paragraph('创建名为 achievement_changes.md 的文件', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('文件格式为有效的markdown', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('包含所有变化内容', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('提供详细的前后对比值', style='List Bullet')

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '实际结果：✓ 全部通过', bold=True)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '两个版本都成功创建了 achievement_changes.md 文件，内容完整。'
        '无技能版本的格式略好，使用了emoji符号（➕、➖、✏️）增强可读性。')

    # ===== 4. 性能对比 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '四、性能对比分析', 1)

    perf_table = doc.add_table(rows=5, cols=4)
    perf_table.style = 'Light Grid Accent 1'

    # 表头
    header_cells = perf_table.rows[0].cells
    headers = ['测试用例', '有技能（秒）', '无技能（秒）', 'Token使用']
    for i, header in enumerate(headers):
        header_cells[i].text = header
        for paragraph in header_cells[i].paragraphs:
            for run in paragraph.runs:
                set_chinese_font(run)
                run.font.bold = True
                run.font.size = Pt(10)

    # 数据行
    data_rows = [
        ['基础对比', '216秒', '84秒', '21k / 19k'],
        ['重点字段', '146秒', '214秒', '24k / 27k'],
        ['生成报告', '61秒', '81秒', '17k / 17k'],
        ['平均值', '141秒', '126秒', '21k / 21k']
    ]

    for i, row_data in enumerate(data_rows, 1):
        row = perf_table.rows[i]
        for j, value in enumerate(row_data):
            row.cells[j].text = value
            for paragraph in row.cells[j].paragraphs:
                for run in paragraph.runs:
                    set_chinese_font(run)
                    run.font.size = Pt(10)

    doc.add_paragraph()

    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '关键发现：', bold=True)
    doc.add_paragraph('整体性能相当：有技能版本平均耗时141秒，无技能版本126秒，差异在合理范围内', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('Token使用效率：两种方式的Token消耗基本相同（约21k）', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('性能波动：个别测试用例存在性能差异，可能与任务复杂度和模型执行路径有关', style='List Bullet')

    doc.add_page_break()

    # ===== 5. 质量评估 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '五、输出质量评估', 1)

    add_heading_custom(doc, '5.1 准确性', 2)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '评分: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (5/5)', bold=True)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '所有测试用例均正确识别了配置表的变化，包括新增、删除和修改的记录。'

    add_heading_custom(doc, '5.2 报告格式', 2)

    add_paragraph_custom(doc,

        '建议改进：可以参考无技能版本使用emoji符号增强可读性。')

    add_heading_custom(doc, '5.3 分析深度', 2)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc, '评分: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (5/5)', bold=True)
    add_paragraph_custom(doc,
        '测试用例2展示了卓越的分析能力，不仅识别了变化，还提供了：'
        '影响评估、设计建议、经济平衡分析、玩家体验考虑等深度洞察。')

    add_heading_custom(doc, '5.4 用户体验', 2)

        '建议改进：增加对git历史的自动获取支持，减少用户手动操作。')

    # ===== 6. 优势与不足 =====
    add_heading_custom(doc, '六、优势与不足分析', 1)

    add_heading_custom(doc, '技能优势', 2)
    doc.add_paragraph('✓ 自动化程度高：无需手动编写对比脚本', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('✓ 专业性强：针对游戏配置表优化，理解业务场景', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('✓ 格式标准化：输出格式一致，易于版本控制和团队协作', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('✓ 可扩展性：支持多种文件格式，易于添加新功能', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('✓ 错误处理：完善的错误提示和引导', style='List Bullet')

    add_heading_custom(doc, '待改进点', 2)
    doc.add_paragraph('⚠ Git集成：尚未实现从git历史自动获取旧版本', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('⚠ 视觉效果：可以借鉴无技能版本的emoji符号使用', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('⚠ 性能优化：部分测试用例耗时较长，可优化执行效率', style='List Bullet')
    doc.add_paragraph('⚠ 配置灵活性：唯一键列的识别可以更智能化', style='List Bullet')

    doc.add_paragraph()

    summary_table = doc.add_table(rows=5, cols=2)
    summary_table.style = 'Medium Shading 1 Accent 1'

    summary_data = [
        ['适用场景', '游戏配置表版本管理、代码审查、发布前检查'],

        ['后续支持', '持续迭代优化，响应用户反馈']
    ]

    for i, (key, value) in enumerate(summary_data):
        row = summary_table.rows[i]
        row.cells[0].text = key
        row.cells[1].text = value

        for cell in row.cells:
            for paragraph in cell.paragraphs:
                for run in paragraph.runs:
                    set_chinese_font(run)
                    run.font.size = Pt(10)

    doc.add_paragraph()
    doc.add_paragraph()

    run = para.add_run('报告生成时间: 2026-02-27\n')
    run2 = para.add_run('测试执行: Claude Opus 4.6\n')
    run3 = para.add_run('文档版本: v1.0')

    for r in [run, run2, run3]:
        set_chinese_font(r)
        r.font.size = Pt(9)
        r.italic = True
        r.font.color.rgb = RGBColor(128, 128, 128)

    para.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER

    # 保存文档
    doc.save(output_path)
    print(f"✓ 报告已生成: {output_path}")
